HAVE_PYCRYPTO = True except Exception: HAVE_PYCRYPTO = False # ---------- Helpers ---------- def _b64e(b: bytes) -> str: return base64.b64encode(b).decode(\"ascii\") def _b64d(s: str) -> bytes: return base64.b64decode(s) def _kdf(password: str, salt: bytes, iters: int = 200_000) -> bytes: if HAVE_PYCRYPTO: return PBKDF2(password, salt, dkLen=32, count=iters, hmac_hash_module=hashlib.sha256) return hashlib.pbkdf2_hmac(\"sha256\", password.encode(), salt, iters, dklen=32) def _aes_gcm_encrypt(plaintext: bytes, password: str) -> dict: salt = os.urandom(16) key = _kdf(password, salt) if HAVE_PYCRYPTO: nonce = get_random_bytes(12) cipher = AES.new(key, AES.MODE_GCM, nonce=nonce) ct, tag = cipher.encrypt_and_digest(plaintext) return {\"salt\": _b64e(salt), \"nonce\": _b64e(nonce), \"ct\": _b64e(ct), \"tag\": _b64e(tag), \"alg\": \"AES-GCM\"} nonce = os.urandom(16) enc_key = key mac_key = hashlib.sha256(key + b\"mac\").digest() out, idx = bytearray(), 0 while len(out) < salt) if container.get(\"alg\") == \"AES-GCM\" and HAVE_PYCRYPTO: cipher = AES.new(key, AES.MODE_GCM, nonce=nonce) return cipher.decrypt_and_verify(ct, tag) enc_key, mac_key = key, hashlib.sha256(key len(out) < len(ct): block = hmac.new(enc_key, nonce + idx.to_bytes(8, \"big\"), hashlib.sha256).digest() out.extend(block); idx += 1 return bytes(a ^ b for a, b in zip(ct, out[:len(ct)])) # ----------
